## <a name="app-startup-errors"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-518">Errori di avvio delle app</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-518">App startup errors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-519">In Visual Studio, per impostazione predefinita un progetto ASP.NET Core usa l'hosting in [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) durante il debug.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-519">In Visual Studio, an ASP.NET Core project defaults to [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) hosting during debugging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-520">Un errore *502,5-Process* o un *errore di avvio 500,30* che si verifica quando il debug locale può essere diagnosticato utilizzando i consigli in questo argomento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-520">A *502.5 - Process Failure* or a *500.30 - Start Failure* that occurs when debugging locally can be diagnosed using the advice in this topic.</span></span>

### <a name="40314-forbidden"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-521">403,14 non consentito</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-521">403.14 Forbidden</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-522">Non è possibile avviare l'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-522">The app fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-523">Viene registrato l'errore seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-523">The following error is logged:</span></span>

```
The Web server is configured to not list the contents of this directory.
```

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-524">L'errore è in genere causato da una distribuzione interruppe sul sistema host, che include uno degli scenari seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-524">The error is usually caused by a broken deployment on the hosting system, which includes any of the following scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-525">L'app viene distribuita nella cartella errata del sistema di hosting.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-525">The app is deployed to the wrong folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-526">Il processo di distribuzione non è riuscito a spostare tutti i file e le cartelle dell'app nella cartella di distribuzione nel sistema di hosting.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-526">The deployment process failed to move all of the app's files and folders to the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-527">Il file *Web. config* non è presente nella distribuzione oppure il contenuto del file *Web. config* non è valido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-527">The *web.config* file is missing from the deployment, or the *web.config* file contents are malformed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-528">Eseguire la procedura seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-528">Perform the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-529">Eliminare tutti i file e le cartelle dalla cartella di distribuzione nel sistema di hosting.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-529">Delete all of the files and folders from the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-530">Ridistribuire il contenuto della cartella di *pubblicazione* dell'app nel sistema host usando il normale metodo di distribuzione, ad esempio Visual Studio, PowerShell o la distribuzione manuale:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-530">Redeploy the contents of the app's *publish* folder to the hosting system using your normal method of deployment, such as Visual Studio, PowerShell, or manual deployment:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-531">Verificare che il file *Web. config* sia presente nella distribuzione e che il contenuto sia corretto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-531">Confirm that the *web.config* file is present in the deployment and that its contents are correct.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-532">Quando si esegue l'hosting in app Azure servizio, verificare che l'app venga distribuita nella cartella `D:\home\site\wwwroot`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-532">When hosting on Azure App Service, confirm that the app is deployed to the `D:\home\site\wwwroot` folder.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-533">Quando l'app è ospitata da IIS, verificare che l'app venga distribuita nel **percorso fisico** IIS visualizzato nelle impostazioni di **base**di **Gestione IIS**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-533">When the app is hosted by IIS, confirm that the app is deployed to the IIS **Physical path** shown in **IIS Manager**'s **Basic Settings**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-534">Verificare che tutti i file e le cartelle dell'app vengano distribuiti confrontando la distribuzione nel sistema di hosting con il contenuto della cartella di *pubblicazione* del progetto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-534">Confirm that all of the app's files and folders are deployed by comparing the deployment on the hosting system to the contents of the project's *publish* folder.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-535">Per ulteriori informazioni sul layout di un'app ASP.NET Core pubblicata, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-535">For more information on the layout of a published ASP.NET Core app, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-536">Per ulteriori informazioni sul file *Web. config* , vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-536">For more information on the *web.config* file, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>.</span></span>

### <a name="500-internal-server-error"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-537">500 - Errore interno del server</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-537">500 Internal Server Error</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-538">L'app viene avviata, ma un errore impedisce al server di soddisfare la richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-538">The app starts, but an error prevents the server from fulfilling the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-539">Questo errore si verifica all'interno del codice dell'app durante l'avvio o durante la creazione di una risposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-539">This error occurs within the app's code during startup or while creating a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-540">La risposta potrebbe non avere alcun contenuto o essere visualizzata nel browser come un codice *500 Errore interno del server*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-540">The response may contain no content, or the response may appear as a *500 Internal Server Error* in the browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-541">Il log eventi dell'applicazione in genere indica che l'app è stata avviata normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-541">The Application Event Log usually states that the app started normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-542">Dal punto di vista del server, questo è corretto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-542">From the server's perspective, that's correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-543">L'app è stata effettivamente avviata, ma non può generare una risposta valida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-543">The app did start, but it can't generate a valid response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-544">Eseguire l'app al prompt dei comandi nel server o abilitare il log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core per risolvere il problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-544">Run the app at a command prompt on the server or enable the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log to troubleshoot the problem.</span></span>

### <a name="5000-in-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-545">500.0 Errore di caricamento del gestore in-process</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-545">500.0 In-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-546">Il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-546">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-547">L'app non viene avviata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-547">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-548">Il [modulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) non riesce a trovare il CLR .NET Core e a trovare il gestore della richiesta in-process (*aspnetcorev2_inprocess. dll*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-548">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) fails to find the .NET Core CLR and find the in-process request handler (*aspnetcorev2_inprocess.dll*).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-549">Verificare quanto segue:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-549">Check that:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-550">L'app specifichi come destinazione il pacchetto NuGet [Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS) o il [metapacchetto Microsoft.AspNetCore.App](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-550">The app targets either the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS) NuGet package or the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-551">Le versione del framework condiviso ASP.NET Core specificata come destinazione dall'app sia installata nel computer di destinazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-551">The version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that the app targets is installed on the target machine.</span></span>

### <a name="5000-out-of-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-552">500.0 Errore di caricamento del gestore out-of-process</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-552">500.0 Out-Of-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-553">Il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-553">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-554">L'app non viene avviata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-554">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-555">Il [modulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) non riesce a trovare il gestore della richiesta di hosting out-of-process.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-555">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) fails to find the out-of-process hosting request handler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-556">Verificare che *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll* sia presente in una sottocartella accanto ad *aspnetcorev2.dll*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-556">Make sure the *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll* is present in a subfolder next to *aspnetcorev2.dll*.</span></span>

### <a name="5025-process-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-557">502.5 Errore del processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-557">502.5 Process Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-558">Il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-558">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-559">L'app non viene avviata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-559">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-560">Il [modulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta di avviare il processo di lavoro, ma l'avvio non riesce.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-560">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the worker process but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-561">La cause di un errore di avvio del processo può in genere essere determinata dalle voci nel registro eventi dell'applicazione e dal log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-561">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-562">Una condizione di errore comune è dovuta alla configurazione non corretta dell'app perché come destinazione viene specificata una versione del framework condiviso ASP.NET Core, che non è presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-562">A common failure condition is the app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-563">Controllare le versioni del framework condiviso ASP.NET Core installate nel computer di destinazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-563">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-564">Il *framework condiviso* è il set di assembly (file *DLL*) che vengono installati nel computer e cui fa riferimento un metapacchetto, ad esempio `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-564">The *shared framework* is the set of assemblies (*.dll* files) that are installed on the machine and referenced by a metapackage such as `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-565">Il riferimento del metapacchetto può specificare una versione minima richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-565">The metapackage reference can specify a minimum required version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-566">Per altre informazioni, vedere [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/) (Il framework condiviso).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-566">For more information, see [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-567">La pagina di errore *502.5 Errore del processo* viene restituita quando il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo a causa di un errore di configurazione dell'hosting o dell'app:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-567">The *502.5 Process Failure* error page is returned when a hosting or app misconfiguration causes the worker process to fail:</span></span>

### <a name="failed-to-start-application-errorcode-0x800700c1"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-568">Non è stato possibile avviare l'aggiornamento dell'applicazione. Errore: 0x800700c1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-568">Failed to start application (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span></span>

```
EventID: 1010
Source: IIS AspNetCore Module V2
Failed to start application '/LM/W3SVC/6/ROOT/', ErrorCode '0x800700c1'.
```

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-569">L'app non è stata avviata perché non è stato possibile caricarne l'assembly ( *.dll*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-569">The app failed to start because the app's assembly (*.dll*) couldn't be loaded.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-570">Questo errore si verifica quando è presente una mancata corrispondenza del numero di bit tra l'app pubblicata e il processo w3wp/iisexpress.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-570">This error occurs when there's a bitness mismatch between the published app and the w3wp/iisexpress process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-571">Verificare che l'impostazione del pool di app a 32 bit sia corretta:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-571">Confirm that the app pool's 32-bit setting is correct:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-572">Selezionare il pool di app in **Pool di applicazioni** di Gestione IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-572">Select the app pool in IIS Manager's **Application Pools**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-573">Selezionare **Impostazioni avanzate** in **Modifica pool di applicazioni** nel pannello **Azioni**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-573">Select **Advanced Settings** under **Edit Application Pool** in the **Actions** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-574">Impostare **Attiva applicazioni a 32 bit**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-574">Set **Enable 32-Bit Applications**:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-575">Se si sta sviluppando un'app a 32 bit (x86), impostare il valore su `True`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-575">If deploying a 32-bit (x86) app, set the value to `True`.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-576">Se si sta sviluppando un'app a 64 bit (x64), impostare il valore su `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-576">If deploying a 64-bit (x64) app, set the value to `False`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-577">Verificare che non esista un conflitto tra una `<Platform>` proprietà MSBuild nel file di progetto e il bit pubblicato dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-577">Confirm that there isn't a conflict between a `<Platform>` MSBuild property in the project file and the published bitness of the app.</span></span>

### <a name="connection-reset"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-578">Reimpostazione della connessione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-578">Connection reset</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-579">Se si verifica un errore dopo l'invio delle intestazioni, è troppo tardi perché il server possa inviare un codice **500 Errore interno del server** quando si verifica un errore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-579">If an error occurs after the headers are sent, it's too late for the server to send a **500 Internal Server Error** when an error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-580">Questo spesso accade quando si verifica un errore durante la serializzazione di oggetti complessi per una risposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-580">This often happens when an error occurs during the serialization of complex objects for a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-581">Questo tipo di errore viene visualizzato come un errore di *reimpostazione della connessione* nel client.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-581">This type of error appears as a *connection reset* error on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-582">La [registrazione delle applicazioni](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) può consentire di risolvere questi tipi di errori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-582">[Application logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) can help troubleshoot these types of errors.</span></span>

### <a name="default-startup-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-583">Limiti di avvio predefiniti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-583">Default startup limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-584">Il [modulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) è configurato con un valore predefinito di *startupTimeLimit* di 120 secondi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-584">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) is configured with a default *startupTimeLimit* of 120 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-585">Quando si mantiene il valore predefinito, l'avvio di un'app potrebbe richiedere fino a due minuti prima che il modulo registri un errore del processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-585">When left at the default value, an app may take up to two minutes to start before the module logs a process failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-586">Per informazioni sulla configurazione del modulo, vedere [Attributi dell'elemento aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-586">For information on configuring the module, see [Attributes of the aspNetCore element](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-587">Risolvere i problemi relativi al servizio app Azure</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-587">Troubleshoot on Azure App Service</span></span>

[!INCLUDE [Azure App Service Preview Notice](~/includes/azure-apps-preview-notice.md)]

### <a name="application-event-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-588">Registro eventi applicazioni (servizio app Azure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-588">Application Event Log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-589">Per accedere al log eventi dell'applicazione, usare il pannello **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi** nel portale di Azure:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-589">To access the Application Event Log, use the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-590">Nel portale di Azure aprire l'app in **Servizi app**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-590">In the Azure portal, open the app in **App Services**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-591">Selezionare **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-591">Select **Diagnose and solve problems**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-592">Selezionare l'intestazione **Strumenti di diagnostica**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-592">Select the **Diagnostic Tools** heading.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-593">In **Strumenti di supporto** selezionare il pulsante **Eventi dell'applicazione**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-593">Under **Support Tools**, select the **Application Events** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-594">Esaminare l'errore più recente dalla voce *IIS AspNetCoreModule* o *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* nella colonna **Origine**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-594">Examine the latest error provided by the *IIS AspNetCoreModule* or *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* entry in the **Source** column.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-595">Un'alternativa all'uso del pannello **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi** consiste nell'esaminare direttamente il file del log eventi dell'applicazione usando [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-595">An alternative to using the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade is to examine the Application Event Log file directly using [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-596">Aprire **Strumenti avanzati** nell'area **Strumenti di sviluppo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-596">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-597">Selezionare il pulsante **Vai&rarr;** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-597">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-598">Verrà aperta la console Kudu in una nuova scheda o finestra del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-598">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-599">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-599">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-600">Aprire la cartella **LogFiles** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-600">Open the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-601">Selezionare l'icona della matita accanto al file *eventlog.xml*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-601">Select the pencil icon next to the *eventlog.xml* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-602">Esaminare il log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-602">Examine the log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-603">Scorrere fino alla fine del log per visualizzare gli eventi più recenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-603">Scroll to the bottom of the log to see the most recent events.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-in-the-kudu-console"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-604">Eseguire l'app nella console Kudu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-604">Run the app in the Kudu console</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-605">Molti errori di avvio non producono informazioni utili nel log eventi dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-605">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-606">È possibile eseguire l'app nella console di esecuzione remota [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) per individuare l'errore:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-606">You can run the app in the [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) Remote Execution Console to discover the error:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-607">Aprire **Strumenti avanzati** nell'area **Strumenti di sviluppo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-607">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-608">Selezionare il pulsante **Vai&rarr;** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-608">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-609">Verrà aperta la console Kudu in una nuova scheda o finestra del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-609">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-610">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-610">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-32-bit-x86-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-611">Test di un'app a 32 bit (x86)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-611">Test a 32-bit (x86) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-612">**Versione corrente**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-612">**Current release**</span></span>

1. `cd d:\home\site\wwwroot`
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-613">Eseguire l'app:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-613">Run the app:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-614">Se l'app è una [distribuzione dipendente dal framework](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-614">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

     ```dotnetcli
     dotnet .\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-615">Se l'app è una [distribuzione autonoma](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-615">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

     ```console
     {ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-616">L'output della console per l'app, in cui sono indicati gli eventuali errori, verrà inviato alla console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-616">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-617">**Distribuzione dipendente dal Framework in esecuzione in una versione di anteprima**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-617">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-618">*Richiede l'installazione dell'estensione del sito del runtime ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-618">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-619">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` è la versione di runtime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-619">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-620">Eseguire l'app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-620">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-621">L'output della console per l'app, in cui sono indicati gli eventuali errori, verrà inviato alla console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-621">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-64-bit-x64-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-622">Test di un'app a 64 bit (x64)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-622">Test a 64-bit (x64) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-623">**Versione corrente**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-623">**Current release**</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-624">Se l'app è una [distribuzione dipendente dal framework](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd) a 64 bit (x64):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-624">If the app is a 64-bit (x64) [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>
  1. `cd D:\Program Files\dotnet`
  1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-625">Eseguire l'app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-625">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-626">Se l'app è una [distribuzione autonoma](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-626">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>
  1. `cd D:\home\site\wwwroot`
  1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-627">Eseguire l'app: `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-627">Run the app: `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-628">L'output della console per l'app, in cui sono indicati gli eventuali errori, verrà inviato alla console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-628">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-629">**Distribuzione dipendente dal Framework in esecuzione in una versione di anteprima**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-629">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-630">*Richiede l'installazione dell'estensione del sito del runtime ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-630">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-631">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x64` (`{X.Y}` è la versione di runtime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-631">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x64` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-632">Eseguire l'app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-632">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-633">L'output della console per l'app, in cui sono indicati gli eventuali errori, verrà inviato alla console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-633">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-634">Log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core (servizio app Azure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-634">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-635">Il log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core spesso registra utili messaggi di errore non disponibili nel log eventi dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-635">The ASP.NET Core Module stdout log often records useful error messages not found in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-636">Per abilitare e visualizzare i log stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-636">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-637">Passare al pannello **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi** nel portale di Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-637">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-638">In **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY** (SELEZIONARE LA CATEGORIA DEL PROBLEMA) selezionare il pulsante **Web App Down** (App Web inattiva).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-638">Under **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY**, select the **Web App Down** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-639">In **soluzioni suggerite** > **abilitare il reindirizzamento dei log stdout**, selezionare il pulsante per **aprire la console Kudu per modificare il file Web. config**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-639">Under **Suggested Solutions** > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection**, select the button to **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-640">Nella **console diagnostica** Kudu aprire le cartelle nel percorso **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-640">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-641">Scorrere verso il basso fino a visualizzare il file *web.config* in fondo all'elenco.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-641">Scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-642">Fare clic sull'icona della matita accanto al file *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-642">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-643">Impostare **stdoutLogEnabled** su `true` e cambiare il percorso di **stdoutLogFile** in: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-643">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-644">Selezionare **Salva** per salvare il file *web.config* aggiornato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-644">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-645">Effettuare una richiesta all'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-645">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-646">Tornare al portale di Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-646">Return to the Azure portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-647">Selezionare il pannello **Strumenti avanzati** nell'area **STRUMENTI DI SVILUPPO**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-647">Select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-648">Selezionare il pulsante **Vai&rarr;** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-648">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-649">Verrà aperta la console Kudu in una nuova scheda o finestra del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-649">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-650">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-650">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-651">Selezionare la cartella **LogFiles**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-651">Select the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-652">Controllare la colonna **Data modifica** e selezionare l'icona della matita per modificare il log stdout con la data di modifica più recente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-652">Inspect the **Modified** column and select the pencil icon to edit the stdout log with the latest modification date.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-653">Quando si apre il file di log, verrà visualizzato l'errore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-653">When the log file opens, the error is displayed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-654">Al termine della risoluzione dei problemi, disabilitare la registrazione stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-654">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-655">Nella **console diagnostica** Kudu tornare al percorso **site** > **wwwroot** per visualizzare il file *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-655">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, return to the path **site** > **wwwroot** to reveal the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-656">Aprire nuovamente il file **web.config** selezionando l'icona della matita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-656">Open the **web.config** file again by selecting the pencil icon.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-657">Impostare **stdoutLogEnabled** su `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-657">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-658">Selezionare **Salva** per salvare il file.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-658">Select **Save** to save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-659">Per altre informazioni, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-659">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-660">La mancata disabilitazione del log stdout può causare un errore dell'app o del server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-660">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-661">Non esiste alcun limite per le dimensioni dei file di log o il numero di file di log che è possibile creare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-661">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-662">Usare la registrazione stdout solo per la risoluzione dei problemi di avvio delle app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-662">Only use stdout logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-663">Per la registrazione generale in un'app ASP.NET Core dopo l'avvio, usare una libreria di registrazione che limita le dimensioni dei file di log e ne esegue la rotazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-663">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-664">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Provider di registrazione di terze parti](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-664">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-debug-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-665">Log di debug del modulo ASP.NET Core (servizio app Azure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-665">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-666">Il log di debug del modulo ASP.NET Core fornisce dati di registrazione aggiuntivi e più approfonditi dal modulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-666">The ASP.NET Core Module debug log provides additional, deeper logging from the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-667">Per abilitare e visualizzare i log stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-667">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-668">Per abilitare il log di diagnostica avanzato, eseguire le operazioni seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-668">To enable the enhanced diagnostic log, perform either of the following:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-669">Seguire le istruzioni in [Log di diagnostica avanzati](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) per configurare l'app per la registrazione di diagnostica avanzata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-669">Follow the instructions in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to configure the app for an enhanced diagnostic logging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-670">Ridistribuire l'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-670">Redeploy the app.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-671">Aggiungere le impostazioni `<handlerSettings>` indicate in [Log di diagnostica avanzati](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) al file *web.config* dell'app distribuita, usando la console Kudu:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-671">Add the `<handlerSettings>` shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to the live app's *web.config* file using the Kudu console:</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-672">Aprire **Strumenti avanzati** nell'area **Strumenti di sviluppo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-672">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-673">Selezionare il pulsante **Vai&rarr;** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-673">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-674">Verrà aperta la console Kudu in una nuova scheda o finestra del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-674">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-675">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-675">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-676">Aprire le cartelle nel percorso **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-676">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-677">Modificare il file *web.config* selezionando il pulsante a forma di matita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-677">Edit the *web.config* file by selecting the pencil button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-678">Aggiungere la sezione `<handlerSettings>` come illustrato in [Log di diagnostica avanzati](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-678">Add the `<handlerSettings>` section as shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-679">Fare clic sul pulsante **Salva**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-679">Select the **Save** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-680">Aprire **Strumenti avanzati** nell'area **Strumenti di sviluppo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-680">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-681">Selezionare il pulsante **Vai&rarr;** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-681">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-682">Verrà aperta la console Kudu in una nuova scheda o finestra del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-682">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-683">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-683">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-684">Aprire le cartelle nel percorso **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-684">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-685">Se non è stato specificato un percorso per il file *aspnetcore-debug.log*, il file viene visualizzato nell'elenco.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-685">If you didn't supply a path for the *aspnetcore-debug.log* file, the file appears in the list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-686">Se è stato specificato un percorso, passare al percorso del file di log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-686">If you supplied a path, navigate to the location of the log file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-687">Aprire il file di log con il pulsante a forma di matita accanto al nome del file.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-687">Open the log file with the pencil button next to the file name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-688">Al termine della risoluzione dei problemi, disabilitare la registrazione di debug:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-688">Disable debug logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-689">Per disabilitare il log di debug avanzato, eseguire le operazioni seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-689">To disable the enhanced debug log, perform either of the following:</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-694">La mancata disabilitazione del log di debug può causare un errore dell'app o del server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-694">Failure to disable the debug log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-695">Non è previsto alcun limite per le dimensioni del file di log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-695">There's no limit on log file size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b3d5-696">Usare solo la registrazione di debug per la risoluzione dei problemi di avvio delle app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b3d5-696">Only use debug logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
